# <a name="edifact-transaction-sets-aperak-iftrin"></a><span data-ttu-id="b4876-102">EDIFACT 交易集 APERAK IFTRIN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b4876-102">EDIFACT Transaction Sets APERAK-IFTRIN</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="b4876-103">本主題列出 BizTalk Server 所支援的 EDIFACT 交易集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b4876-103">This topic lists the EDIFACT transaction sets that are supported by BizTalk Server.</span></span>

-   [<span data-ttu-id="b4876-107">交易集 CNTCND CONAPW</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b4876-107">Transaction Sets CNTCND-CONAPW</span></span>](../core/edifact-transaction-sets-aperak-iftrin.md#cntcnd)  
  
-   [<span data-ttu-id="b4876-108">交易集 CONDPV CONWQD</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b4876-108">Transaction Sets CONDPV-CONWQD</span></span>](../core/edifact-transaction-sets-aperak-iftrin.md#condpv)  
  
-   [<span data-ttu-id="b4876-109">交易集 COPARN CREMUL</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b4876-109">Transaction Sets COPARN-CREMUL</span></span>](../core/edifact-transaction-sets-aperak-iftrin.md#coparn)  
  
-   [<span data-ttu-id="b4876-110">交易集 CUSCAR DEBREC</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b4876-110">Transaction Sets CUSCAR-DEBREC</span></span>](../core/edifact-transaction-sets-aperak-iftrin.md#cuscar)  
  
-   [<span data-ttu-id="b4876-111">交易集 DELFOR DOCADV</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b4876-111">Transaction Sets DELFOR-DOCADV</span></span>](../core/edifact-transaction-sets-aperak-iftrin.md#delfor)
